 During this time, some parts of the body often have pain: 1
 peeth main dard honisedoraan peeth main dard hona bahut aam he
 This happens because the uterus is growing in the womb, which makes the front part very heavy
 pet baari ho jane kii vajah se peeth main jhukaav aana shuru ho jaataa he
 This causes pain in the back almost daily
 2
 Feet pain: During pregnancy, the upper body weight of the woman increases significantly
 jisase uske pairon par bahut adhik bhaar padane lagata he
 The bones are not able to bear this weight and because of this, there is always pain in the legs
 3
 Headache: There is heaviness in the head every morning during pregnancy
 iskaa pramukh kaaran ye bhi hota he ki is dauraan neend aniyamit ho jaati he
 In such a situation, headaches often occur due to lack of sleep and hormonal changes
 4
 Pain in the breast During this time, many hormonal changes occur due to which the breasts become big and hard
 jisaki vajah se unamem aksar dard bana rahata he
 5

 In the hot summer of Odisha, the election campaign there is at full speed
 raajnneetik prishthbhumirenkanal loksabhaa seat par congress or biju janata dal kaa prabhutv rahaa he
 Janta Dal, Swatantra Party and Republic Council candidates have been winning this seat from time to time
 1952 main is seat par congress candidet niranjan jena ne jeet hasil kii
 In 1957 Surendra Mohanty of Republic Council won the elections
 1962 main ye seat congress ke kabje main ai
 In 1967, Swatantra Party opened an account on the seat
 1971 main yahaan se congress ke devendra satpathi ko vijay shri hasil hui
 In 1977, when there was a wave against the Congress in the country, Devendra Satpathy joined the Bharatiya Lok Dal and won elections on this seat
 1980-84 main dhenkanal seat par congress kaa kabja rahaa
 Kamakhya Prasad Singh Dev won the election both times
 kamakhya prasad singh dev sthaneey raaj parivaar ke sadsy hai or unke parivaar kaa is seat par prabhutv he
 In 1989, there was a wave of change and the public won
 lekin 1991 main congress ke tikat par kamakhya dev ne phir vaapasi kii
 He also won in 1996
 1997 ke aakhri dinon main biju janata dal ke gathan ke baad is seat kaa sameekaran badal gaya
 The Tathagata Satpathy of the Congress emerged victorious in the 1998 Lok Sabha elections
 haalanki 1999 main jab chunaav hue to congress ne yahaan jeet hasil kii
 Since 2004, the Biju Janata Dal has strengthened its hold on this seat
